.pcfactory-fade-enter,
.pcfactory-fade-appear {
  animation-duration: 0.2s;
  animation-fill-mode: both;
  animation-play-state: paused;
}
.pcfactory-fade-leave {
  animation-duration: 0.2s;
  animation-fill-mode: both;
  animation-play-state: paused;
}
.pcfactory-fade-enter.pcfactory-fade-enter-active,
.pcfactory-fade-appear.pcfactory-fade-appear-active {
  animation-name: antFadeIn;
  animation-play-state: running;
}
.pcfactory-fade-leave.pcfactory-fade-leave-active {
  animation-name: antFadeOut;
  animation-play-state: running;
  pointer-events: none;
}
.pcfactory-fade-enter,
.pcfactory-fade-appear {
  opacity: 0;
  animation-timing-function: linear;
}
.pcfactory-fade-leave {
  animation-timing-function: linear;
}
@keyframes antFadeIn {
  0% {
    opacity: 0;
  }
  100% {
    opacity: 1;
  }
}
@keyframes antFadeOut {
  0% {
    opacity: 1;
  }
  100% {
    opacity: 0;
  }
}

[pcfactory-click-animating='true'],
[pcfactory-click-animating-without-extra-node='true'] {
  position: relative;
}
html {
  --antd-wave-shadow-color: #5C8CFC;
  --scroll-bar: 0;
}
[pcfactory-click-animating-without-extra-node='true']::after,
.pcfactory-click-animating-node {
  position: absolute;
  top: 0;
  right: 0;
  bottom: 0;
  left: 0;
  display: block;
  border-radius: inherit;
  box-shadow: 0 0 0 0 #5C8CFC;
  box-shadow: 0 0 0 0 var(--antd-wave-shadow-color);
  opacity: 0.2;
  animation: fadeEffect 2s cubic-bezier(0.08, 0.82, 0.17, 1), waveEffect 0.4s cubic-bezier(0.08, 0.82, 0.17, 1);
  animation-fill-mode: forwards;
  content: '';
  pointer-events: none;
}
@keyframes waveEffect {
  100% {
    box-shadow: 0 0 0 #5C8CFC;
    box-shadow: 0 0 0 6px var(--antd-wave-shadow-color);
  }
}
@keyframes fadeEffect {
  100% {
    opacity: 0;
  }
}

/**
 * 控件（组件）样式文件
 * 各组件基本遵循最外层被以 “ued-xxx-wrap" 为样式名的容器包裹，模拟局部css作用域
 *
 * 为什么不直接在组件内部以 css module 的方式引入样式？
 * 答：1. 因为在打包构建时，各模块包裹容器的样式名会加上hash编码
 * 2. 今后如果想实现动态主题变更，就需要在线编译less样式，而编译时需要有一份基准数据
 * 3. 如果是以组件内部的样式文件内容作为基准数据，里面的样式名是没有进行hash编码过的，会与构建后的文件匹配不上，就算生成新的css，也不会生效
 * 4. 所以基准数据大概率会包含此文件内容（入口文件还会含有 antd 库中原生样式内容），通过less，替换里面的less变量，生成新的css，插入到html中，做到样式变更
 * 优点：每个组件模块的样式名都是约定的，不会在构建过程中加上hash编码
 */
